);

    username STRING NOT NULL,
    email STRING NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP
);


CREATE TABLE tasks (
    task_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    task_name STRING NOT NULL,
    project_id INT REFERENCES projects(project_id),
    assigned_to INT REFERENCES users(user_id),
    due_date DATE,
    status STRING
);
